120 2022-05-29/00:30:19 174 insert into wrh$_comp_iostat (dbid, per_pdb, con_dbid, snap_id, instance_number, COMPONENT, FILE_TYPE, IO_TYPE, OPERATION, BYTES, IO_COUNT) select :dbid, 0 per_pdb, :srcdbid con_dbid, :snap_id, :instance_number, 'RMAN', 'DATAFILE', is_sync, type, sum(bytes), sum(io_count) FROM (select :dbid, 0 per_pdb, :srcdbid con_dbid, decode(x.type, 1, 'READ', 'WRITE') as type, case when (bitand(x.flags, 2) = 0) then 'SYNC' e lse 'ASYNC' end as is_sync, x.blocks * x.block_size as bytes, case when (bitand(x.flags, 2) = 0) then (x.sync_count) else (x.async_short_count + x.async_long_count + x.async_ready) end as io_count FROM x$ksfqp x, v$dbfile df WHERE (1 = 1) and x.type in (1,2) and df.name = x.filename) awsubq$1 GROUP BY is_sync, type
